ARIE vol.039, 1916-1917


A.--List of copper-plates examined during 1916-17.
1
Placement
The Sub-Collector, Bezwada(Kistna district).
Year
Eastern Chā-ḷukya.
King
Amma (II)
Date
Uttarāyaṇa
Language and Script
Sanskrit
Remarks
Records the gift of the village Māṅgallu inNātavāḍi-vishaya to the Brahmaṇ Dommana,at the instance of Kākartya-Guṇḍyana, sonof E1ṟiya-Rāshṭrakūṭa and grand-son ofGuṇḍiya-Rāshṭrakūṭa of the Sāma[nta]voḍḍifamily.
2
Placement
M.R.Ry. Velpula Raghavulu,Yeddanapudi (Narasarao-pet taluk, Guntur district).
Year
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1637,Manmatha,Āshāḍha, śu.5.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Registers the sale of their mirāśi-inām landsby the brothers Vīrātattuḍu and Yallā-battuḍu of Yaddanapūḍi, for ga, 275 (varā-hālu). By this the services of blacksmithto the Sircar (government) were transferredto the purchaser Vēlpūri Musalābattuḍu inthe presence of 9 witnesses.

…

Language and Script
Kanarese
Remarks
Sale of Gauḍika-mirāśi lands by Timmana-Gauḍa and Gōvinda-Gauḍa of Maḍḍiliṅga-dahaḷḷi, to Timmaṇa-Gauḍa of Yisibe, to-gether with pasiki, paḷige, mūlavīsa, aṅgaḍi-vīḷyavartans, yīḷige, piñjāṟṟu, kāḍārambha,nīrārambha, etc., belonging to those lands,for 25 ga. (varāha).

Remarks
The first plate is missing and the writing isvery carelessly executed. There are manyomissions and ??-spellings. Registers thegift of a village surnamed Veṅkaṭēśapurain the Kōnāḍu district, a sub-division ofUttukkā[ḍu]-Kōṭṭam, to the Śrī-Vaishṇavateacher Tātaya the grand-son of E1ṭūr-Tātār-ya and son of Śrīnivāsa.

13
Placement
Do. do.
Year
…
King
…
Date
…
Language and Script
Nāgarī
Remarks
These two plates (without ring) are written onfour sides in two different types of character.The bigger letters (of perhaps a later date)belong to the time of Kalyāṇakaḷaśa [Nētri-bhañja] and commence and close like hisGumsūr copper-plates published with textand translation in Journal of Bengal AsiaticSociety, Vol. 6, pages 667 to 671. Thesmaller characters are of the same type asthose of the Buguḍa plates of Mādhavavar-man and begin similarly (Epigraphia Indica,Volume III, p. 41 f., and ibid. Volume VII,p. 100 f.). The former is a palimpsest.

17
Placement
Tahsildar of Madakasira(Anantapur District).
Year
…
King
…
Date
…
Language and Script
Nāgarī (Kanarese)
Remarks
In Śālivāhana-Śaka 1230, Plavaṅga, Kārttikaśu. 15, solar eclipse (?), the gauḍike of thevillage Dēvarāyapura to Sādara Muddumallawas made by Tirumala-Sōmayājin. Thelatter had received it as dīkshārā makshētrafrom the king Gaḍḍada Dēvarāya. Theāyagāras for the new village were appointedin the presence of the residents of fourvillages. The village seems to have beensurnamed Roḷe.
18
Placement
Do.
Year
…
King
…
Date
…
Language and Script
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers that, in Śaka 1120, Bhāva (wrong) acertain Bomma-Nāyaka with the permissionof Harihara-Bukkarāya appointed kāṇachi-gāras (i.e., village servants) in the villageMādasamudra which he had founded. Thenin Śaka 1223, Naḷa (also wrong) in the reignof Bhūpatirāya, son of Harihara-Bukkarāya,Bomma's son Kāma-Nayaka founded to thesouth of Malligemaḍu the village Gōvinda-pura which he renamed Rorḷe.
19
Placement
Do.
Year
Vijayana-gara.
King
Vīrapratāpa Vīra-Śrī-Raṅgarāyadēva-Mahārāya.
Date
Śaka 1578,Viḷambi(wrong), Mā-gha, śu. 15.
Language and Script
Kanarese
Remarks
A quarrel regarding the gauḍike of Roḷebetween Annadāni-Gauḍa and Chiga-Mudhaiya was submitted to the (village) court(dharmāsana) consisting of the chief men ofthe village and the twelve village servants(āyagāra). They decided in favour of thelatter and the chief Sarajarāyapparāja ofHarati accepted their decision and conferredthe gauḍike on Mudhaiya.

The members of the village (ūr) who performed the Śēnāpati-ttaṉam and daṇḍanāyakam and the tandirattār whobelonged to the parikkiragam of Kōnāḍu-Kaḍayam aliasVikrama-Pāṇḍyanallūr gave their maintenance (jīvita)-lands under Āṇḍārkuḷam to Daśaratha-Rāmīśvaramuḍaiyārin the temple of Śrī-Kailāsam of that village in order that theworship and offerings to the several gods and goddesses setup by them in that temple may be conducted. In doingthis, the temple was required to pay some money to threedifferent mortgagees and to get the release of the lands.The donors agreed to pay Iñjadu and variñjaduon these lands by reserving for themselves 1 kalam ofpaddy on each mā of wet-land on which crops had beenraised.

ANANTAPUR DISTRICT MADAKSIRA TALUK
1
Placement
On a pillar set up in the court yard of theRaṅganāthasvāmin temple at Palla-banda.
Year
Vijaya-nagara.
King
Vīrapratāpa Sadāśivarāya-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1478, NaḷaPushya, śu.di. 8.
Language and Script
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers that under orders of the Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Rāma-rāju-Tirumalarājayyadēva-Mahā-arasu, the Mahānāyaka-āchārya Timmaṇa-Nāyaka of Niḍugal and the gauḍa andsēnabōva residents of that province together with the mer-chants, gave Tūmukuṇṭe in Niḍugala-rājya to the temple ofTiruveṅgaḷanātha at Peyyalabaṇḍe for offerings, worshipand festivals. The gift was actually made on the 11th day.Mentions Keñchappa-Nāyaka the mudre-officer of Gutti-Tirumalarājayyadēva-Mahā-arasu evidently the same asRāmarāja-Tirumalarājayyadēva mentioned above.

Damaged. Registers that Immaḍi Timmaṇa-Nāyaka ofNiḍugallu gave the kāṇāchi of the tank Narasāmbudhi-kuṇṭe to a certain Samani Pāpaya with the permission ofthe god Tiruveṅgaḷanātha of Peyakoṇḍe, since this Pāpayawas regularly every year erecting a pandal (chapara) in thename of Peyalakoṇḍa Raṅganātha, was going on pilgrimageto Tirumale every year and was repairing the chapara athis own cost.

40
Placement
On a pillar set up in the courtyard of theJaina temple in the same village.
Year
…
King
Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara TribhuvanamallaNiśśaṅkapratāpachakravarti Vīradā-nava-Murāri, Iruṅgoṇadēva-ChōḷaMahārāja of the Chōḷa race ‘ruling atthe capital town of Niḍugallu.’
Date
Śaka 1200, Īś-vara, Āshā-ḍha, śu. di.pañchamī,Monday.
Language and Script
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers that Malliseṭṭi son of Saṅgayana-Bommiseṭṭi andMēḷavve and the favourite lay disciple of Bāḷēndu-Mahadhāri-dēva who was the senior pupil of Tribhuvanakīrtirāvuḷa ofIṅgaḷēśvara, of Mūla-saṅgha, Dēsiya-gaṇa, Koṇḍakund-ān-vaya and Pustakayagachchha, gave at Tammaḍihaḷḷi the2,000 areca trees which belonged to his share, to Prasanna-Pārśvadēva of the basadi of Tailaṅgeṟe known as Brahma-Jinālaya. The priest of this temple was Challapiḷḷe aJina-Brāhmaṇa of Bhuvalōkanāthanallūr in Bhuvalōka-nātha-vishaya, a sub-division of Ponnamarāvati-sīme, northof Dakshiṇa-Madhurā in the southern Pāṇḍya country.From the produce of this garden land śampūrṇavāhanawere to be constructed of stone, the basadi from its upānato stūpi, the mahā-maṇḍapa, bhadrā, Lakshamīmaṇḍapa,gōpura, enclosere (parisūtra), festoons (vandanamāle),Mānastambha and makaratōraṇa.

187
Placement
On a slab set up near the Śiva temple atMadipadu (same taluk, same district).
Year
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1582, Śār-varin, Mā-gha, Śiva-rātri.
Language and Script
Telugu & Sanskrit
Remarks
Mentions a number of Paramahaṁsa-parivrājakāchāryas ofwhom the first was Kṛishṇāśrama; next came Rāmabha-drāśrama; then Raghurāmāśrama; then Rāmagōpālā-śrama and then Pūrṇābhinava Raghurāmāśrama-Śrīpāda.This teacher Raghurāmāśrama-Śrīpāda consecrated thetemple of Rāmēśvara on the bank of the Kṛishṇā andone of Dakshiṇamūrti under the bēl-tree there and putup this śāsana for the good of the varṇāśrama-pilgrims. Itis stated that Prauḍha-Dēvarāya was cured of his leprosyby a bath at this holy spot. It describes the greatness ofthe place quoting a story from the Skānda-purāṇa that eventhe holy river Ganges was purified of the heinous sin ofhaving come into contact with a Brāhmaṇa window thatassociated with a chaṇḍāla, by drinking and bathing at thisholy spot where the Kṛishṇā flows northward.
